         function msieversion(){
             var ua = window.navigator.userAgent;
             var msie = ua.indexOf ( "MSIE " );
 
             if ( msie > 0 ) {
                 return parseInt (ua.substring (msie+5, ua.indexOf (".", msie )));
             } else {
                 return 0;
             }
         }

 function fillItems(intStart) {
 
     var makeSel = document.getElementById('make');
     var modelSel = document.getElementById('model');
 
     var a = modelItems;
 
     var b, c, d, intMake, intModel
 
     if ( intStart > 0 ) {
         for ( b = 0; b < a.length; b++ ) {
             if ( a[b][1] == intStart )
                 intModel = a[b][0];
         }
 
         for ( c = 0; c < makeSel.length; c++ ) {
             if ( makeSel.options[ c ].value == intMake )
                 makeSel.selectedIndex = c;
         }
     }
 
 
     if ( intMake == null )
         intMake = makeSel.options[ makeSel.selectedIndex ].value;
 
     modelSel.options.length = 0;
 
     modelSel.options[ modelSel.options.length ] = new Option('Any model', 0);
 
     for ( d = 0; d < a.length; d++ ) {
         if ( a[d][0] == intMake )
             modelSel.options[ modelSel.options.length ] = new Option( a[d][2], a[d][1] );
 
         if ( a[d][1] == intStart )
             modelSel.selectedIndex = modelSel.options.length - 1;
     }
 	
 	
 	try {
 		var priceSel = document.getElementsByName('price')[0];
 		priceSel.style.visibility = 'hidden';	
 	}
 	catch (e) 
 	{
 		//alert(e);	
 	}
     try {
         var fuel_type = document.getElementsByName('fuel_type')[0];
         fuel_type.style.visibility = 'hidden';
     }
     catch (e)
     {
         //alert(e);
     }
 }

     window.addEventListener('load', function(){
     function sticky_relocate() {
        var window_top = $(window).scrollTop();
        var div_top = $('#nav-trigger').offset().top;
        if (window_top > div_top) {
          // Navigation
          $('#primary-navigation').addClass('stick');
        } else {
          // Navigation
          $('#primary-navigation').removeClass('stick');
        }
    }
 
    $(function () {
        $(window).scroll(sticky_relocate);
        sticky_relocate();
   });
   });
    </script>

    <script>
     window.addEventListener('load', function(){
   function sticky_relocate() {
       var window_top = $(window).scrollTop();
       var engageTrigger = $('#engage-trigger');
       if(engageTrigger.length){
         var div_top = engageTrigger.offset().top;
         if (window_top > div_top) {
           // Navigation
           $('#detail-engage').addClass('stick');
         } else {
           // Navigation
           $('#detail-engage').removeClass('stick');
         }
       }
   }
 
   $(function () {
       $(window).scroll(sticky_relocate);
       sticky_relocate();
 });
 });
    </script>

    <script>
     window.addEventListener("load", function () {
 
 
       var active_id = 0;
       var tracking_id = 0;
       var element_id = 0;
 
       $('html').click(function (e) {
           var myClass = $(e.target).attr("class");
           if (myClass != "responsive-img") {
               $(".person-info").hide();
           }
       });
 
       $(".person").click(function () {
           if (element_id[1]) {
               $("#personinfo-" + element_id[1]).hide();
           }
 
           active_id = this.id
           element_id = active_id.split("-")
 
           var tracking_id = "#personinfo-" + element_id[1]
 
           $("#personinfo-" + element_id[1]).show();
       });
 
       // $( "#promo-expander" ).click(function() {
       //   $( "#promo-expand" ).slideToggle( "slow", function() {
       //     // Animation complete.
       //   });
       // });
   });
    </script>
